<div id="review_243258085" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243258085" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243258085?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243258085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8825924906572614781">REVIEW COMPLETED SEPTEMBER 6, 2012<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"You'll get the good stuff, Duchess."</i>
</b> <b>Wonder Max. Divine.</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/?action=view&current=DanielVilla4.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379772567i/309373._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Admittedly, my Max did change his eye color from grey to brown. Whatever. He is gorgeous.<br/><br/><i>"Forgot about carin' about someone so much you would do everything in your power to stop them havin' pain."</i><br/><br/>I should have read <i>The Gamble</i> sooner rather than later. Yes, <i>Sweet Dreams</i> and Tate will always stay above and beyond, however, Max…he is simply another divine KA hero. I was surprised that he had very few </span>
  <span id="freeText8825924906572614781" style="display:none">REVIEW COMPLETED SEPTEMBER 6, 2012<br><br><b>
  <i>"You'll get the good stuff, Duchess."</i>
</b> <b>Wonder Max. Divine.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/?action=view&amp;current=DanielVilla4.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379772567i/309373._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Admittedly, my Max did change his eye color from grey to brown. Whatever. He is gorgeous.<br><br><i>"Forgot about carin' about someone so much you would do everything in your power to stop them havin' pain."</i><br><br>I should have read <i>The Gamble</i> sooner rather than later. Yes, <i>Sweet Dreams</i> and Tate will always stay above and beyond, however, Max…he is simply another divine KA hero. I was surprised that he had very few jerk<i>-ish</i> moments, and I felt that he was kind of tamer than her other badass alphas.<br><br><i>"You're being domineering again," I informed him.<br>I felt his mouth grin under mine and watched his eyes do it.<br>"Yeah, baby, fair warnin', when we're naked, you better get used to that."<br>I gasped at his words then he kissed me.</i><br><br>Without a shadow of a doubt scrumptious, studtastic, yet caring and tender Max is responsible for another unforgettable read. Max challenged Nina. He made her think and kept her on her toes. Max is the opposite of boring, that's for sure, and Wonder Max offered me another wonderful taste of KA sweet. Mmmm…Max is sex on a stick! And while we're on it, the sex was good, however, for such a loooong book I'd've appreciated some more smexy times. Whatever. Despite that <i>The Gamble</i> is not a perfect book, there is always something very specific that I can find in every KA story: a feel of utter contentment after having read one of her novels. Kristen is able to make me want to devour her stories and characters. Yet again, she left me wanting more.<br><br><i>"I'm not making out with you in a bar."<br>"Why not?"<br>"Why?"<br>His face again dipped closer. "Because first I want you to. And second whether you believe it or not, guys are checkin' you out and that'd be me stakin' my claim."<br>"Staking your claim?"<br>"It's a guy thing."<br>"It's a Macho Mountain Man thing."<br>"Same thing."<br>"You're impossible."<br>"You gonna kiss me or what?"<br>"If I don't you're just going to kiss me anyway, aren't you?"<br>Again, he gave me a grin. "You finally got that?"<br>"Impossible," I muttered.<br>"Kiss me, Duchess."</i><br><br>Where this book did not quite work for me was the heroine. I'm very sorry to say it but Nina has to be one of KA's most annoying heroines. She was simply too neurotic and hysterical for me. That said, she was always so wrapped up in her own drama and neuroses that she never gave enough thought about what Max was going through. I've had my issues with her jumping to conclusions all the freakin' time, and when did she actually ask Max about the stuff that bothered her? I mean why is it so difficult to voice what you'd like to know? Now and then I silently told her "Just spill it already!!" I think Nina has a hearing defect 'cause she did not listen to me. Having said that, she was listening to other people's insights and was jumping to conclusions again. Yeah, and then when Max laid it all out to dear Nina…hell, what did she do, huh? She was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[running away. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> *pulls hair out* Nina, just get your head sorted! Further, I really didn't appreciate it that she had to tell me what Max was thinking or feeling or how he'd react. Bottom line: she was very exhausting. <br><br>Now that my Nina rant is over, let me say something positive about this heroine. Nina had some terrific moments. When Mindy tried <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[to commit suicide, Nina gave everything she had to save her life.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And their conversation after this "incident" was very thoughtful and heartwarming. It really touched me in a major way. Lovely.<br><br><i>It was then I wondered if things would have felt differently if Max had been around when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Charlie died. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> If I'd have had this, maybe not the view, but his strong arms around me, his cheek to my hair. If I'd had him to hold onto.</i><br><br>I really liked Brody, Mindy, Cotton, Nellie and Steve (Nina's mom and stepdad). As always the cast of secondary characters was amazing. Kristen brought them to life and they simply clicked for me.<br><br>From time to time I had to suspend belief a little bit, especially when Nina <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[flew into the windshield and hardly hurt herself. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Right, this is fiction and I have to live with it. What grated on my nerves as well was the screeching, shrieking, and crying (shouting). Let's just say that less is more. Then again, I couldn't help but enjoy it and shake my head when the bunch of crazy yet endearing people cracked me up.<br><br>Kristen writes the very best epilogues--ever. Max was holding <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[their super cute baby in his lap. Yeah, Max, I'm going to let you borrow my very own cutie pie 'cause I know you're going to take care of him. &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3<br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/miscellaneous/?action=view&amp;current=Scan.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364347i/716008._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>And then at the end this specific scene...<br><br><i>I'm happy for you, honey,</i> Anna said and Max closed his eyes.<br>Then he opened them and pulled Nina closer.<br>"I'm happy too," he whispered.<br><i>I'm going now. If Nina asks where he's gone, tell her I'm taking Charlie with me.</i><br>Max didn't answer.<br><i>I love you, Max, and I love the way she loves you.</i><br>She would love that, Anna would. That was pure Anna.<br>"Find peace, Swanee," Max replied.<br><i>Already did, 'bout three years ago, baby.</i><br>Max's jaw clenched to fight against his throat getting tight. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Yeah, my throat got very tight. Beautiful.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8825924906572614781" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1110443405" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1110443405" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1110443405?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18246040-the-gamble">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110443405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7442258666306938026"><b>4 the definition of guilty pleasure STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416420991i/11961673.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And another <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> book for me. I simply can't stop with this woman. I'm guessing it has something to do with my current mood and my need to read something lovely that makes me feel good...like coming home, or eating comfort food in grandma's kitchen.<br/><br/>Anyway...why did I put 'the definition of guilty pleasure' up there in my rating? Because it's one of those chick flicks where you have to suspend your disbelieve and just go with the flow.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7442258666306938026" style="display:none"><b>4 the definition of guilty pleasure STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416420991i/11961673.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And another <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> book for me. I simply can't stop with this woman. I'm guessing it has something to do with my current mood and my need to read something lovely that makes me feel good...like coming home, or eating comfort food in grandma's kitchen.<br><br>Anyway...why did I put 'the definition of guilty pleasure' up there in my rating? Because it's one of those chick flicks where you have to suspend your disbelieve and just go with the flow.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I looked to the ceiling and told God, “God, next time I want an adventure, strike me with lightning. You have my permission.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Thirty-six year old <b>Nina Sheridan</b> needs a timeout from her job and her life, but most importantly from her neglecting fiancé. So naturally she hops on a plane from England to America, drives into the Colorado Mountains where she booked a beautiful A-Frame for two weeks.<br><br>Turns out the idyllic get-away is occupied by the owner and her booking was made by mistake. Said owner, <b>Holden "Max" Maxwell</b> makes her turn around in a snow storm to find a hotel room in town. What could possibly go wrong, right?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When I met you, my first thought was you were very pretty, great fuckin' eyes, but not my type. High-class which means high maintenance. Then you got pissed and that was it. Even if you hadn't been in that ditch, now you'd still be in my bed. So if you think this attitude is a turn off, baby you're wrong.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Just a minor accident. Nina lands in a ditch and wakes up in the A-Frame...rescued by Max. *sigh*<br><br>The moment she hit that snow bank I jumped up and down and screamed...OMG she's about to be rescued by someone tall, dark and handsome...See where I'm going with the whole cliché, guilty pleasure, suspend your disbelieve thing?<br><br>No?<br><br>Well, I'll give you one more thing. <br><br>Turns out Nina gets sick...honest to god...fever and not being able to walk sick. Max takes care of her and after she is better he won't let her leave...o.O I mean he is sweet about it and there is a spark there and they go into town and do stuff and have guests over and all that, but common sense says ...RUN, girl...RUN!<br><br>Remember? Suspend your disbelieve!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You think to slide back, settle for something that made you run away because you think it's safe, because it's familiar, because your scare of taking a GAMBLE on me, I'm warning you now, Duchess, I'm not gonna allow that.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>If you just go with the flow, this is one hell of an entertaining book. The whole town is involved and is cheering for Max and Nina and there are a lot of crazy mountain town people shenanigans going on and oh...there's a murder. <br><br>Didn't expect that, did you?<br><br>Then there is also the matter of the fiancé and family is always a bad thing and thank god for pretty mountain views...life would be really hard otherwise. ;P<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Babe,” he replied, grinning then said no more. Still being helpful, I explained, “I know you think that word speaks volumes but, I have to tell you, it actually doesn’t.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>My biggest problem was Nina. She is a smart woman, a lawyer, and she is very independent and self sufficient and all that. But for some reason she doesn't talk in whole sentences. Here are her favourite words: <i>'Um...' 'Max.'</i> and my personal favourite...<i>'Sorry?'</i><br><br>I think she has some hearing problems. Nina doesn't get what you're saying the first time around, which is odd since she is a smart girl. But in the end it leads to people always repeating their sentences to her...Ugh and that's just not cool.<br><br>But Max on the other hand is AWSOME!! He's all -mountain man, no bullshit, I take what I want and I take care of what I own- fabulous. It's pretty neat, in a romance book kind of way.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re being domineering again,” I informed him.<br>I felt his mouth grin under mine and watched his eyes do it. <br>“Yeah, baby, fair warnin’, when we’re naked, you better get used to that.”<br>I gasped at his words then he kissed me.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>So, Max the local poster boy who everyone loves and the American girl who lived too long in England and who speaks in an English accent. They're the best. OMG, they fight...mostly because Nina is a hell cat and Max is a stubborn mountain man and they bicker and they are made for each other. From the moment they met there was no other way but for them to be a couple...fate really. ;D<br><br>I'm going to read the first book in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/69394-the-burg" rel="nofollow noopener">The ‘Burg</a> series next...just hopping around and checking out all of KA's books and different scenarios. I'll be back to the Colorado Mountains in no time.<br><br>See you then. ;D<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_241924718" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/241924718" />
    <a title="Ana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1316580-ana"><img alt="Ana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491291179p2/1316580.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/241924718?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ana" href="/user/show/1316580-ana">Ana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1316580-ana?shelf=zz-read-in-2012">zz-read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1316580-ana?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer241924718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4995120470664510237">Nina Sheridan desperately needed a timeout from her life (especially her fiancee). So spending a week in a rented A-Frame in the Colorado mountains sounds like haven.<br/><br/>Unfortunately, when she gets there she has a nasty surprise. The owner changed his mind and is staying in the house.<br/><br/>And to top it all, her car went into a ditch and she has a nasty flu. A great start, no? And that's just the beginning.<br/><br/>Nina was an OK heroine, I liked her. She's feisty, argumentative, has a pretty bad temper, and she'</span>
  <span id="freeText4995120470664510237" style="display:none">Nina Sheridan desperately needed a timeout from her life (especially her fiancee). So spending a week in a rented A-Frame in the Colorado mountains sounds like haven.<br /><br />Unfortunately, when she gets there she has a nasty surprise. The owner changed his mind and is staying in the house.<br /><br />And to top it all, her car went into a ditch and she has a nasty flu. A great start, no? And that's just the beginning.<br /><br />Nina was an OK heroine, I liked her. She's feisty, argumentative, has a pretty bad temper, and she's hell on wheels when upset. But she's also sweet and kind, and incredibly helpful to those she likes. Her life so far has been one trial after another, and her vacation is no exception:<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>...but I don’t know why you want me. It’s mad.”<br /><br />“Nina –”<br /><br />“I mean, I go on a vacation to try to figure out my life and here I am, my leg’s scraped up, my ribs are bruised, I’ve been backhanded and punched, I’ve been to a hospital once and a Police Station three times and I’ve been into it with practically everyone in town and, if you take out the time I’ve been sick, I’ve only been here a week!”<br /><br />“Duchess, let me –”<br /><br />“What is it with me?” I asked over him then again didn’t wait for an answer, just kept blathering. “I need a timeout to deal with my timeout! That’s how messed up I am. And you’re a good guy, the best, you take care of people, everyone respects you, you’re nice and you’re handsome and you’re generous and smart and you don’t need all that is messed up me messing up you.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Luckily, coming to Gnaw Bone (that's the name of the town, I'm not kidding), seems to be one of the best decision's she made in her life.<br /><br />Max, what to say about Max. He's a great guy. Generous, steady, willing to help anyone and everyone. His personal life took a hit 10 years ago, but he didn't get out of rails (except when it comes to women). And now there's Nina (AKA Duchess). She's irresistible. <br /><br />He can be a Neanderthal (actually he is one most of the time), and autocratic as well, but he means well, so I can forgive him that.<br /><br />I like how their relationship developed. The flirting, bantering - it was incredibly amusing. But they shared the painful stuff as well. And mostly they opened up to each other as well.<br /><br />The setting as well, the Colorado Mountains...<br /><br />I like the people of Gnaw Bone, they are so unique. And Nina's mother is incredible. Love that woman.<br /><br />There were some problems with the editing. I noticed some mistakes, and there were sentences that I simply didn't get even after rereading them. It's not that bad, but if you can't stand them, this may not be the book for you.<br /><br />The reason for the 4 star rating is mostly Nina. Her behavior towards the end started to irritate me. I understand her issues and fears, but she was sabotaging their relationship, simply kept waiting for a reason to leave. <br /><br />And the book was long. I even think too long. There's so much stuff crammed in, that it became a bit ridiculous at times.<br /><br />All in all, I liked the book and I will be reading the sequel <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227040.Sweet_Dreams__Colorado_Mountain___2_" title="Sweet Dreams (Colorado Mountain, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams</a>.<br /><br />Rating:<br /><br /><b>4.5 stars</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4995120470664510237" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1657504358" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1657504358" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1657504358?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18246040-the-gamble">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1657504358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14947936131926196690"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You think to slide back, settle for something that made you run away because you think it's safe, because it's familiar, because you're scared of takin' a gamble on me, I'm warnin' you now, Duchess, I'm not gonna allow that."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>4 Holden Maxwell Stars!</b><br/><br/>Be still my heart. This book was all kinds of sweet and adorable and wonderful!<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_' title='The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Gamble</a> may be wordy but it was so worthy. 670+ pages and I regret nothing! Perhaps it has something to do with the way the author made me feel so ooey and g</span>
  <span id="freeText14947936131926196690" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You think to slide back, settle for something that made you run away because you think it's safe, because it's familiar, because you're scared of takin' a gamble on me, I'm warnin' you now, Duchess, I'm not gonna allow that."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>4 Holden Maxwell Stars!</b><br><br>Be still my heart. This book was all kinds of sweet and adorable and wonderful!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gamble</a> may be wordy but it was so worthy. 670+ pages and I regret nothing! Perhaps it has something to do with the way the author made me feel so ooey and gooey inside all throughout the book and how she provided such an atmospheric depiction of Colorado Mountain.<br><br>The story started when English heroine <b>Nina Sheridan</b> went to Colorado Mountain for a vacation-slash-timeout. She was confused with what's going on with her relationship with her fiancé and she needed a moment to think. In order to do that, she has to go somewhere far and cozy and Colorado Mountain was perfect for it. The moment she stepped into the beautiful mansion she's supposed to stay, she met the handsome (or should I say, perfect) owner named <b>Max</b>. While staying there they were able to get to know each other and well, eventually developed attraction and fell in love. Of course it wasn't that perfect and easy since Nina's already engaged and Max has a complicated past that she has to find out.<br><br>I found this book quite a guilty-pleasure. I'm a first-time Kristen Ashley reader and I couldn't help but admire her delicious writing. She has this way of engaging her readers through her entertaining characters and romantic, sexy innuendos. Max was literal Alpha-Male. He was a jealous and possessive caveman but I couldn't help but fall in love with his character. While Max was sometimes a jerk, Nina was the exact opposite. She was soft but she's a tough one. Not to mention she was cute and funny. The two of them totally made a great couple and yes, they're now my favorite sweethearts.<br><br>There were lots of conflicts in this book and while I found some of them quite unnecessary, such as Mindy's personal dilemmas, I think they added a little bit of spice to the story. There were also lots of misunderstandings between Max and Nina but they were resolved and I was happy with that. <br><br>One thing that made me appreciate this book was Nina and Max's relationship which felt real to me. They both have imperfections but they've willingly accept them. They also made some mistakes but they corrected them and didn't let them become a reason to let each other fall apart. The give and take relationship amazed me.<br><br>And now here's my favorite line from Max to Niles:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Fucked her last night, man, and this morning. Five times. Five. It was like she hadn’t been touched in a decade. So fuckin’ sweet. Damn,” he taunted, his eyes locked on Niles. “You’ve had her, you gotta know, not enough money in the world’s worth that."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br><i>Yes. Be still my heart...</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gamble</a>, as a whole, was a beautiful start to the series. After reading it, I decided to read more books written by Kristen Ashley. She has so many novels that were recommended to me by my lovely friends. Do you fancy winter romance books? Then put this on your tbr. :)<br><br><p>

  </a>
</p><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer402287040" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7796950300880756169"><b>4 Please stop saying you're sorry before I hit you stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389312i/750361._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><b>
  <i>"You lose anyone, there’s no replacing them. What you need to get is that's precious. You get to keep that. You don't want to replace it. That doesn't mean you can't find something else just as good."</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389312i/750362._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389135i/750132._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Welcome to Gnaw Bone, Colorado. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380756296i/3120093._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>I'm not sure why I spent my time searching through pictures to find my perfect Max and Nina, where really, I could have just gone with <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380756296i/3120094.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>(Did I just age myself?) <br/><br/>I love, and I mean LOVE Kristen Ashley books. </span>
  <span id="freeText7796950300880756169" style="display:none"><b>4 Please stop saying you're sorry before I hit you stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389312i/750361._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>
  <i>"You lose anyone, there’s no replacing them. What you need to get is that's precious. You get to keep that. You don't want to replace it. That doesn't mean you can't find something else just as good."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389312i/750362._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389135i/750132._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Welcome to Gnaw Bone, Colorado. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380756296i/3120093._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I'm not sure why I spent my time searching through pictures to find my perfect Max and Nina, where really, I could have just gone with <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380756296i/3120094.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>(Did I just age myself?) <br><br>I love, and I mean LOVE Kristen Ashley books. I have no idea how I managed to read every book in the Colorado Man series BUT this one. Really. I'm still trying to figure that out. Obviously I've been a bad bad girl, and Max need to punish me...thoroughly... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417132ra/824739.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But I digress. After reading a few of KA's recent books, my first thought when I started reading The Gamble? THIS! This is KA at her finest. Damn but I missed her. Don't get me wrong, I've enjoyed her recent books, but it always felt a little off. So it was so great to get my KA fix with Max and Nina. What did I love the most about The Gamble? <br><b>Max</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380756296ra/3120095.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The man was perfect! No seriously friggin perfect! He said things like this<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Learned some things in my life, Duchess, one of the most important, you find a good woman, you take care of her." <br>"Please." <br>"This happens between us, Duchess, I'd take care of you." <br>"Don't." <br>"Die doin' it," he vowed.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He was growly and possessive and I just wanted to lick him! What? It's this thing I get with growly and possessive heroes. You don't? Huh. But then there was Nina<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425951ra/850494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Now I know I tend to have a short fuse when it comes to irritating heroines...but FOR THE LOVE OF ALL THAT'S HOLY she worked my last damn nerve. Here we have a 36 year old woman, a professional lawyer, and most of the time she acts like a teenager. Yes she was sassy when it came to standing up for herself and I liked that. But when it came to Max? GAH!<br><br>I mean here we have a situation that can easily be resolved by talking it through. Max is willing to talk it out with her. Max even pretty much begs to talk things out with her. Yet every single time instead of talking it out, she just jumps to her own stupid conclusions. The other times she stews on it, gets mad and takes it out on Max, or just runs.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380756296ra/3120096.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Here you have this amazing, sexy, growling man that for some god unknown reason wants your crazy ass. Yet all you do is give him shit, more shit, and then dish up shit some more. I ask you <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/635781.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Though to be fair, I would have been fine with all that. If I could give Nina just one handy dandy little thing. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380756296i/3120097.jpg" alt="" width="171" height="220" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Please, for the sake of my sanity, Nina, look up the word "sorry". I'm sure there will be something in there. It felt like most of her vocabularly when it came to Max consisted of: "I'm sorry", "Um", and "Uh". <b>GAH!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380756296ra/3120098.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story itself was fantastic. I loved the mystery, suspense, and full out drama. All the side characters and their stories were great too. I love how KA can include a few side character plots without it getting muddy or confusing. The who-done-it ending caught me by complete and utter surprise. I did not see it coming at all. <br><br>Then there was the epilogue. *GUSHING* No one and I mean NO ONE can write an epilogue quite like KA. And this one was no exception. Nina was definitely not a favorite heroine of mine, but luckily the book was still THAT good that I was able to more or less tolerate her. So that is all the heroine bashing you will be getting from me. And I thank you <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755439.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Though now I'm feeling the sudden urge to re-read this entire amazing series. *dreamy sigh*<br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a></span>

<div id="review_1553928664" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1553928664" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1553928664?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=buddy-read-with-bbbs">buddy-read-with-bbbs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=read-while-cutting-onions">read-while-cutting-onions</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1553928664" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11478873504586053438">I've never actually watched one of those Lifetime movies that are dramatic and sappy, but I imagine that this is what they are like. Along with an improbable romance, there are kidnappings, suicide attempts, bar fights, abusive men, murders, and alien babies. (okay, maybe not the alien babies. Too bad because that would have been awesome! oh, oh, how about alien twin babies and one of them is an evil twin? Yes! I love evil twins!)<br/><br/>This book is about Nina, an American girl who has spent most of he</span>
  <span id="freeText11478873504586053438" style="display:none">I've never actually watched one of those Lifetime movies that are dramatic and sappy, but I imagine that this is what they are like. Along with an improbable romance, there are kidnappings, suicide attempts, bar fights, abusive men, murders, and alien babies. (okay, maybe not the alien babies. Too bad because that would have been awesome! oh, oh, how about alien twin babies and one of them is an evil twin? Yes! I love evil twins!)<br><br>This book is about Nina, an American girl who has spent most of her life in England and is engaged to a boring guy who doesn't care about her, and Max, an alpha Colorado mountain man who owns the cabin that Nina rented to get away from it all and decide if she really wants to marry Mr. Boring Dud. (I'm guessing "no".)<br><br>Nina shows up at her rental cabin and finds out that there was a mistake and the owner, Max, is at home. He's a dick, she leaves, and promptly crashes her car into a ditch. Thanks a lot for making us women drivers look bad, Nina!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456013835i/18180361._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I bet she makes a great sandwich, though...</i><br><br>Max saves her, and immediately she gets sick, so he keeps her at the cabin and nurses her back to health.<br><br>Okay, that's really sweet, BUT, he also decides to undress her - including her bra, while she is asleep, to <i>help</i>. Ummm, dude, are you a nurse? Is my bra being on life-threatening? No? Then, hands-off motherfucker! No verbal consent means no touchy the goodies!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456013835i/18180362.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Interestingly enough, Max has many young female friends that he considers like sisters to him. Why didn't he call one of them over to undress a woman he doesn't know who is definitely wearing an engagement ring? Hmmmm, good question. I don't want to call him Chester the Molester or anything, but... well, I just did. I can live with myself.<br><br>Max must have liked the merchandise that he so creepily leered at while Nina was unconscious because when she is well, he tells her that he has taken the keys to her rental car and will not allow her to leave. He also called the only taxi service in town and told them not to pick her up if she called for <s>help</s> a ride. And, as I mentioned, this cabin is in a remote area of the woods....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456013835i/18180363.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Director: this is the perfect setting for a cutesy rom-com!</i><br><br>Isn't this romantic? Don't answer that. Because, you see, Max is hot, so this is all good. If he were old or ugly, this would be horrible and terrifying. But, he's hot. So,,,,, you know. It's cute and sweet - not a felony kidnapping and sexual molestation charge.<br><br>Okay, but this is Kristen Ashley. All of her books have this kind of thing going on. It's fiction. <br>I just have to keep reminding myself of this and then I can enjoy her books. Because, the woman sure does write some great characters, funny dialogue, and hilarious situations. If you can get past the almost criminally pushy main male characters, you will have a blast reading her books.<br><br>Will I keep reading her books? Probably. <br>Will I keep complaining about the overbearing alpha males that she writes? Definitely. <br>What can I say? I apparently like to complain. Who knew? (Don't answer that!)</span>
  <a data-text-id="11478873504586053438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8827002850110634204" style="display:none"><b>Re-read (on audio) for the 3rd time May 21st 2018 and loved it all over again. I'm changing my 4 star rating to 5 star! <br /><br />Re-read (on audio) April 22nd 2015<br /></b><br /><br />Just as good if not better the second time around. This is classic Kristen Ashley with all the rambling and crazy, fun friends. Of course wouldn't be KA without a delicious Alpha male who won't let go or take no for an answer. <br /><br />Emma Taylor does an excellent job with Nina's English accent. Max calling Nina "Duchess" made even more sense hearing her accent. <br /><br /><b>December 25th 2012</b><br />Well, this was a lot of fun! Can I have my own <b>Colorado Macho Mountain Man?!!</b> Max was a typical Kristen Ashley Alph-Male, but isn't that what we love about her writing? Domineering, possessive, growly, and of course, 100% HOT!! <br /><br />Nina was a cutie and I loved her big heart. This poor girl got knocked around a fair amount. I would say Daemon paid dearly, though. The secondary characters were loads of fun and provided extra entertainment throughout. This story was long but I never felt it lost my attention. KA definitely knows how to write an addictive story that will have you clicking through pages, oblivious to all that surrounds you. <br /><br />Favorite quote:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I lucked out, baby," Max went on. "When I was young life handed me somethin' beautiful. Then it took it away. Ten years down the road, somethin' different, but no less beautiful, showed up right at my front door. I knew it almost the minute I saw it and nothin' has happened since to shake that. You think, findin' that in you, I'm gonna let you change my password, write me some f&amp;%ked up note and walk away?" </i>
</b><br /><br /><i>A copy was provided by Grand Central Publishing through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review. Thank you.</i></span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_632711811" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/632711811" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/632711811?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Kristen Ashley Fans, Romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17755575-wendy-sthoughts?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer632711811" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8766614394547738474"><b>5 Rolling the Dice Stars<br/>* * * * * <i>During these times in 2020 of Cray Cray, I decided I needed Max and Nina. The OG Ashley will always be a draw for me. </i><br/>❤️❤️❤️ ❤️❤️❤️ ❤️❤️❤️ ❤️❤️❤️<br/><i>Spoiler Free-Full Review 2013/2018</i><br/>Once Upon a Time, I discovered Kristen Ashley. I was new to Goodreads and never had any idea I would ever start reviewing. I just had heard about Ashley and the only way to get her books were as an Ebook. I went to Amazon, got the Kindle App, and then my addiction started. I was hooked </b></span>
  <span id="freeText8766614394547738474" style="display:none"><b>5 Rolling the Dice Stars<br>* * * * * <i>During these times in 2020 of Cray Cray, I decided I needed Max and Nina. The OG Ashley will always be a draw for me. </i><br>❤️❤️❤️ ❤️❤️❤️ ❤️❤️❤️ ❤️❤️❤️<br><i>Spoiler Free-Full Review 2013/2018</i><br>Once Upon a Time, I discovered Kristen Ashley. I was new to Goodreads and never had any idea I would ever start reviewing. I just had heard about Ashley and the only way to get her books were as an Ebook. I went to Amazon, got the Kindle App, and then my addiction started. I was hooked from the start and over a few weeks I read everything I could get my hands on... I even would risk reading at work...Not just at lunch... but at my desk, on the work computer!<br><br>I loved them all and just gave them ratings from the heart... But man, oh, man....Max was special. <br><br>Recently I saw The Gamble was FREE and all of the wonderful memories of reading it for the first time came flooding back...Endorphins, light-headiness, and just the silly grin I could not wipe off my face.<br><br>I am not an authority of Kristen Ashley in any shape or form...but I do have an appreciation of her talent and publishing arc. For those who would like to find Like-Minded Lovers of Ashley, Goodreads has a group aptly titled, Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492-kristen-ashley-addict-s-support-group">https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/...</a><br><br>From what I could find on the web, her book Rock Chick was self-published in 2008. She had tapped into a need for fun, flirty, sexy reads with her own independent twist. She took the idea of women being friends, a little reckless...daring and paired it with romance that was like no other.<br><br>Her woman was strong... clear-headed and willing to go to the mat for her friends. It was sometimes this side of goofy in parts but all of it had heart and swoon-worthy moments that were off the charts. And this new author with her style of describing everything.... homes, decor, clothing, and inner dialogue was fresh and liked...<br><br>A Lot.<br><br>She proceeded to publish in 2009 and 2010 a new entry to the series each year.<br><br>Then 2011 happened and all hell broke loose! Ashley published a total of 21 books... all of different series and types of romance. She covered fantasy, suspense, paranormal, and motorcycle brotherhood. She gave her original series 4 more books. She had to have been working on all of these projects during her quiet years because of the volume of work produced.<br><br>Which leads me to The Gamble. This was a release during Ashley's Golden Year of 2011. It was the first book in a new series based in a small town Gnaw Bone, Colorado. It had the allure of the concept of Mountain Men who were dominant but not in an ugly way... there was this charm in their need to protect, handle things and be committed to what they saw was right...and the trick was they were correct, too.</b><br><br>The story opens with a woman in flux...Nina Sheridan is re-thinking her engagement to a man who seems to not listen to her when she speaks or never has time to take her calls because the meeting or project he is about to do is much more important. But with all Nina has gone through in her life...she thought safe and polite was the way to go...but she now was feeling the boredom, how what said was not counting and mostly...how alone and lonely she was. She explained to her fiancee she was going to leave England and go back home to the States, for a two week Time Out to evaluate everything. Nina even told Niles she was not feeling that great when she left...but it seems to have fallen on deaf ears...once again.<br><br>Nina had decided she needed an adventure and when she saw this beautiful A-Frame in the Colorado Mountains online with views to take the breath away...she reserved it, paid upfront, and was now driving to the location through a snowy night. Nina took the time to buy groceries and supplies and only wanted to climb into bed and crash. She had flown 17 hours with her body telling her a cold of some kind was coming. When she saw the actual A-frame ...it was more beautiful than the pictures. She hoped the man who opened the door as she approached was the realtor.<br><br>Holden "Max" Maxwell was not expecting anyone. As the owner of the house he was kicking back having a beer and relaxing. Then this beautiful, well-dressed woman is walking in boots that have too high a heel and no business being in snow. As she comes closer to the door, she calls out and her accent clearly sounds British.<br><br>Nina is asking him if he is the realtor and the next thing she knows he is telling her no and to go on her way...Well, that won't do, not at all. With flashing eyes and a strong stance, Nina informs him she has paid for the A-Frame in advance, wants to get her groceries, luggage and supplies into the house and settle.<br><br>As Max takes all of this in, he is on the phone letting the realtor know he messed up big time. Max rents out the house when he is on construction sites and somehow Nina was confirmed for this time. Max hangs up the phone and tells Nina to turn around, go to town and there is a very nice motel where she can stay.<br><br>Words are exchanged, first with Nina standing her ground...then with her feeling worse and Max seeing she is not the best, he offers her to stay since the night is getting later and the snow heavier. Nina now will not admit anything to Max and stomps out to her car, muttering how she wanted an adventure...well remind her to never come to Colorado to have one.<br><br>Nina tries to go down the hill to the road but gets stuck in a ditch. She has no strength to do anything but go to the trunk, put on every of clothing she could find, take the cold medicine she bought in Denver and climb into the back seat to sleep. She would worry about the car tomorrow.<br><br>Nina opens her eyes barely, as the pain is so great, and doesn't understand where she is...and when she figures out it is a comfy bed with soft sheets and comforter, she tries to feel for her clothes...only to feel a t-shirt and panties on her body, a body which aches and hurts from her cold...<br><br>Max makes an appearance and Nina wants to fuss and fight but is too sick to do it for too long...Max had checked after a while to see if Nina had reached the motel and then became concerned when no one had seen her anywhere. He found her in the ditch, out to the world and carried her and all of her stuff back to the house. Now he is looking at Nina and sees she is running a fever and needs to take more medicine.<br><br>This Mountain Man, someone Nina has never experienced, is doing more for her then the man she was supposed to marry.<br><br>This is the setup and Boy, oh, Boy...what a tale. You have these two people and each has their own backstory which will rip your heart out...but not to worry because by these two coming together...all will be JUST FINE...<br><br>Now Max is a man any woman in their right mind would want...I am not going to go into a whole thing...I am going to let you meet him for yourself and bask in the glory of Max.<br><br>I will share, though, that he has the ability to get his point across and not like many other Ashley Men, speaks in complete sentences. They may be a bit short or direct to the issue...but what he says is clear and so Max. Max also is a man who knows how to love up a woman...and Ashley is the best in how she creates the scenes, dialogue, and feel of every touch and caress. The chemistry Nina and Max together is strong and true. What works so well is the fact that Max is a toucher...he touches his woman, holds her, leans into her, wraps his arms around her front to his back...and man...can he kiss. Ashley shows all the ways to take readers right into the moment, feel everything that was happening but never crossing into an awkward or clumsy coupling.<br><br>Nina is also a strong character with all the quirks and issues Ashley is known for ...Nina has pain from a loss of her brother and there is a past history of bad choices in men...so her default is to expect the worst. She has to work to see what Max is and is not...<br><br>There is so much in this book with people figuring out they are worth love and then accepting it. Ashley addresses the need for those who have experienced traumatic events getting the help they need and being open to sharing their pain before it becomes too much. There is more, too..but what really worked was how every event was structured to make sense...not just thrown in there for the excitement.<br><br>As I said in other reviews of Ashley, I have always felt this series had more depth and intensity than many of her earlier ones. The layers of crafting, the way the plotting worked on all levels was impressive. I know there are many fans of Max and Nina and hopefully, new ones will be coming.<br><br>This was another re-read of this book and won't be my last... <br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1327890208l/11227041._SX50_.jpg" alt="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <b>The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/632711811">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a <div id="review_485024978" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/485024978" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/485024978?book_show_action=true">Dec 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to * Meli Mel * by: </span>
      Melissa *Pervy Kitten* and Tessa Teevan
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=uber-sweet">uber-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=female-pov">female-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=hells-yeah-alphas">hells-yeah-alphas</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485024978" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3190801255132745907"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 5 'Macho Mountain Man' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780788._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='250' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>The Gamble</i> takes place in a small town named Gnaw Bone, Colorado. This is the place Nina Sheridan goes to for a "timeout" from her fiancé Niles. When she arrives at the cabin she rented, she meets Max, the owner of the Cabin. Max only rents out the cabin when he isn't home, so there has been a mix up. He pretty much kicks her out of the cabin and tells her to go to a hotel. Nina gets pissed off then storms away only to get stuck in the snow and fall sick. Max </span>
  <span id="freeText3190801255132745907" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 5 'Macho Mountain Man' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780788._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>The Gamble</i> takes place in a small town named Gnaw Bone, Colorado. This is the place Nina Sheridan goes to for a "timeout" from her fiancé Niles. When she arrives at the cabin she rented, she meets Max, the owner of the Cabin. Max only rents out the cabin when he isn't home, so there has been a mix up. He pretty much kicks her out of the cabin and tells her to go to a hotel. Nina gets pissed off then storms away only to get stuck in the snow and fall sick. Max finds her and takes care of her during her illness. He agrees to have her stay, and as time goes by, they start to fall for each other. But their lives are disturbed by the events that are occuring in town. One being a murder of man Max knew, and him being a suspect.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780789._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“You just need to know, I gotta fight to keep what we got so we can build on it, I will. Him, your Dad, you, I don’t give a fuck. In my life, I’ve learned when to let shit go and when to fight. This, babe, what we got, I’ll fight for.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>My sweet, sweet <b>Holden 'Max' Maxwell</b>... how I LOVED him. I want to be sick just so I can have him take care of me.... *sigh*. I melted with the way he cared for Nina while she was ill. He was domineering and very much an Alpha but it was never overbearing. He was super loving and I just wanted to kiss him for it. He took care of almost everyone in that town in some way. I loved the kisses to the forhead, him calling Nina "Duchess" and just pretty much anything he would do. And he does what every girl wants from her man... HE FREAKING LISTENS!! He made me swoon at how he remembered all the small things that had to do with Nina. He had a tragic past though, and still, he was kind and didn't stay bitter about what happened. I loved that he showed Nina how it's like to be in a relationship where she matters. He was just perfect... *dreamy smile* LOVED HIM!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780790._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"There was a time in my life where I used to roll the dice. I did it a lot and I always lost. Every time, I lost and when I lost, I lost everything. So I got scared of rolling the dice. Thank you for showing me it was worth taking a gamble again, darling. It feels good to finally win and win huge."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I really liked <b>Nina 'Duchess' Sheridan</b>. She was definitely a feisty nut but I loved that she had some backbone. This girl can really stand up for herself, even when she's facing someone bigger and scarier. She will defend those she cares about. She leaves England and her dumbass fiancé to find herself, to figure out her wants. I loved that even though her past was not a walk in the park either, she remained strong. Yes she had a shield, but she was still very loving to those around her. I'm so glad Max was able to breakdown her barrier because together they were so freaking adorable. I love how independent she was and how she supportive she was of Mindy. She was an amazing friend. I just loved her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401972ra/780791.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their romance was definitely what had me glued to this book. But I was also quite interested with what was going on with the case of the murder of Curtis. I wanted to know who did it. It was like freaking clue, and I love that game. I suspected a person and then I was SO shocked to find out who the killer really was. I had quickly dismissed this person and that person ended up being it. What also had me interested was the story with Mindy and Jeff. I was so happy for her, she's been through so much and all I wanted was for her to be blissfully happy. I'm glad she found that with Jeff. Niles... He was a friggin' idiot!...Nuff said. Damon... I just wanted to castrate him... Nuff said. Shauna... I hated the bitch... Nuff said. Kami was a bitch in the beginning, and in a way, I'm glad she had to go through all that she did in order for her to see the light. She may not be 100% bitch free, but she became better. I loved Nina's family, especially her mom, she was a hoot. I also love how Kristen Ashley incorporated Nina's brother, Charles into the story, that was awesome!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401972ra/780792.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“You know, I do too,” I heard his gravelly voice rumble quietly.<br><br>“What?” I asked his throat.<br>He didn’t answer and when his silence lasted a long time, I lifted my head and looked down at his face to see he looked sated and serious.<br>“What do I know?” I queried.<br><br>His fingers stopped their roaming, one arm locked around my waist, the other hand slid up my spine and into my hair. His amazing gray eyes didn’t leave mine when he answered gently, “I do too. I said it the other day and I meant it.” His fingers tensed against my scalp. “I’m in love with you, Duchess.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The ending was great. I liked how everything was resolved. But what I absolutely LOVED, was the epilogue. It was so adorably sweet. I had the hugest smile and a few tears. I loved it! I actually wanted to know more about Mindy and Jeff. But I am so happy with the HEA. I LOVED Max, I was surprised I really liked the heroine and the story was really entertaining. The only thing I could complain about would be the length. It was so long! But still, I really enjoyed it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3190801255132745907" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

This, babe, what we got, I’ll fight for.” </i> </b><br/><br/>The Gamble was my second ever Kristen Ashley novel. I think I discovered it on a random listopia list here on Goodreads. This, babe, what we got, I’ll fight for.” </i> </b><br><br>The Gamble was my second ever Kristen Ashley novel. I think I discovered it on a random listopia list here on Goodreads. This is the book where I fell in love with her as an author, and I devoured the Mountain Man series. I've never read another series like this one, and I don't think I ever will.<br><br>I love Max and his Duchess. Such a wonderful story of a lost woman who found herself with the help of the right man. The plot is a little crazy yeah, but just fall into it and the fantasy and you'll love it.<br><br>My only criticism and why it's a 4 and not a 5 even after a reread is it's way too long. But otherwise it's wonderful.<br><br><b> <i> “Learned some things in my life, Duchess, one of the most important, you find a good woman, you take care of her.” <br>“Please”<br>“This happens between us, Duchess, I’d take care of you.”<br>“Don’t”<br>“Die doin’ it,” he vowed.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>

If you are a reader who enjoys Ms. Ahsley's style of writing; then this will be a book you will highly enjoy. A great addition </span>
  <span id="freeText6475937555019752534" style="display:none">This was another great Kristen Ashley read.. I did however find it somewhat long.   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/372212948" />
    <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward"><img alt="Kellie Maddox-Ward" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366371073p2/7309666.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

I forgot how friggin good this story was!<br><br>So, this is me (and my husband) moving 'our last daughter' (we have 4) on this fine Labor Day weekend to Ottawa University into residence (because we live 4 hours away). My husbands driving, my daughters listening to her I-pod, and I'm reading this bloody book's epilogue and bawling my eyes out. <br><br><br>My husband just looks at me and shakes his head (because I've been reading a lot of books lately that have had me in tears... <i>{thank you very much KA!}</i>). <br><br>I finished this book with such a warm-fuzzy feeling because I TOTALLY forgot how friggin HOT Holden Maxwell was, and how much I liked Nina character! <br>Their chemistry was off the charts.<br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pictures%203/tonguekiss.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>AMAZING! AMAZING! AMAZING!<br><br><br><b>Third re-read: Finished July 26, 2014</b><br>Still one of my favourites!<br><br><br><b>Fourth re-read: September 16-18, 2017</b><br><br>Wow! I hadn't realized it had been 3 years since I last read this book.<br>This is the book where it all begins. <br>Where we (the readers) are introduced to these incredibly strong, mountainous, domineering, protective, smart Colorado Mountain Men.<br>Loved this re-read!<br>Once again the characters were amazing to read and get to know all over again.<br>It's funny, I just re-read this whole series over the last month and I was saving this book (the first book in the series) for the last because it was the first book I ever read by Kristen Ashley, the one that got me hooked, and it's still one my favourites.<br><br><b>Fifth re-read December 10-11, 2018</b><br>Damn!<br><br><a href="https://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/truelovephoto-1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
