<div id="review_424920984" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/424920984" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/424920984?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=amazing-sexual-tension">amazing-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=fave-authors">fave-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=hea">hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=great-surrounding-characters">great-surrounding-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=rape">rape</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=steamy-reads">steamy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=action-drama-full-reads">action-drama-full-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer424920984" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17290794298391500879"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756299._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756300._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>As usual, Kristen Ashley doing what she does best! Hot, sexy, dominant, protective alpha males. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756301.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5 stars for Nina and Max!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756302._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756303._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book is long. To be honest, this was a bad week for me to read it as I had lots going on outside of my 'reading world'... but it's been sitting on my Kindle for ages and I just really felt the need for a good KA hero. And despite the length of this book, it does not drag. At all! It's fast paced, action packed and I wouldn't have wanted it to be any shorter.<br/><br/>The story is t</span>
  <span id="freeText17290794298391500879" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756299._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756300._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As usual, Kristen Ashley doing what she does best! Hot, sexy, dominant, protective alpha males. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756301.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5 stars for Nina and Max!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756302._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756303._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is long. To be honest, this was a bad week for me to read it as I had lots going on outside of my 'reading world'... but it's been sitting on my Kindle for ages and I just really felt the need for a good KA hero. And despite the length of this book, it does not drag. At all! It's fast paced, action packed and I wouldn't have wanted it to be any shorter.<br><br>The story is that Nina Sheridan has escaped to the Colorado Mountains for a time out from her inattentive, unexciting fiancée, Niles. She intends to give herself time to think and work out whether marrying Niles is what she really wants or not, whether she wants the safe, monotonous life she was built for herself after a history of bad relationships, or whether there is more to life. But before she can get any thinking time done, Nina meets Max. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Macho Mountain Man Max</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756304.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holden Maxwell owns the A-frame that Nina has rented for her little getaway. There's been a mistake and Max is home, so the A-frame shouldn't have been rented at all. Within minutes of meeting Nina and the gorgeous, but moody Max are arguing and Nina storms out into the snowstorm, heading for the nearest hotel. A series of events lead to Nina ending up back at the A-frame with Max and that is where she stays.<br><br>But this is a KA book, so obviously, that isn't all that happens. The town of Gnaw Bone is thrown when the local bad-guy is murdered and everybody becomes a suspect. On top of that, Max's friends and family all have their own issues to deal with and before she knows it, Nina is embroiled in the lives of these people that she barely knows. <br>Of course, as time goes on, Max decides that despite their initial spat, he rather likes Nina and tries to convince her to stay. So amongst all of the drama, Nina has to decide whether she wants to return to her humdrum life in England or take a gamble on Holden Maxwell and his mountain!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You think yo slide back, settle for something that made you run away because you think it's safe, because it's familiar, because you're scared of takin' a gamble on me, I'm warnin' you now, Duchess, I'm not gonna allow that."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756305.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Phew... that's a long story short...<br><br>As you'd expect from a KA book, <i>The Gamble</i> is laced with murder, kidnapping, villains, punch-ups and mystery. So much happens in this book. I love Kristen's writing. She's so clever, the way she builds a story, develops all of the surrounding characters, keeps the mystery flowing throughout the book to create a fantastic, frantic, 'I'd-never-have-predicted-that' climax. Obviously, with all Kristen Ashley's books, the drama is all completely over the top. Completely nuts. But completely great! It's kind of almost comical, how far fetched KA's story lines, but it just works with the whole feel of her writing, the characters, etc.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756306.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Amongst all the shootings, betrayal and crime fighting, there's a deliciously sexy romance. Nina and Max's chemistry is off the charts hot. It isn't all that graphic and it is most definitely secondary to everything else that is going on this book, but there were times when I thought my Kindle might start smoking. Max is a dirty-talker, ladies. *fans self* He's so sensual and confident, so determined and sure of what he wants, and that in itself is so scrummy.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>And then Max really kissed me and I became so lost, I never wanted to be found.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756307._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nina is brilliant. She's sassy and ballsy. But she's also incredibly defensive. She's been through some terrible relationships. She's been cheated on, lied to, beaten and she's lost people she loved. She's erected high, impenetrable walls to keep herself safe from any more hurt and Max struggles to break these down. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Maybe she thinks she's not worthy. You want her, man, your job is to convince her she's wrong."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>However, she's hilariously confrontational. In the week she is at Gnaw Bone she has it out with just about everybody living there. It's brilliant when her mouth runs away with her and her hackles are raised. And I loved Max's reaction to this, too.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756308.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, Max. Gorgeous. Absolutely, one percent, gorgeous hunk of man meat. Like most of KA's heroes, he's completely and utterly everything that defines 'Alpha male'. He's a little bit moody, a whole lot controlling, very over protective, has a sexy, gravelly voice, cuts her off in the middle of sentences, calls her babe, honey, sweetheart and Duchess, melts her with a hand on the back of her neck... he's ripped, sexy as hell, spends a lot of time brooding and I luuuuurve him! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756309._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756310.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's the perfect mix of strong and sensitive. And who doesn't love a man who can admit when he's wrong? ;) I loved that Max was always so in control. Even when he was mad, he was still mostly uber cool and calm. His fierce protectiveness is swoonworthy and overall, he was impossible not to fall in love with.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This happens between us, Duchess, I'd take care of you."<br>"Don't."<br>"Die doin' it," he vowed.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>If you've read Kristen Ashley books before, you'll know exactly the type of book boyfriend I'm talking about. You can spot a KA book hero a country mile off... and they're just as delicious every single time. If you <i>haven't</i> read KA books and you like yourself some super sexy Alpha man-candy... you need to get on it! <br><br>She writes her characters so well. You can really feel the body language, the tone of voice, the facial expressions. She brings her characters to life in every single book. And each one has their own little defining features, little ways about them, catch phrases, words or nicknames they use, habits in the way they move... she individualises each of them so skilfully. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756311.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Her writing is so easy to read, it just rolls right off the page. She writes as you would speak and it makes the book so relatable. You really feel like you are inside the head of the character. She's a storyteller through and through.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Babe," he replies, grinning then said no more.<br>Still being helpful, I explained, "I know you think that word speaks volumes but, I have to tell you, it actually doesn't."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And then there are her epilogues. KA executes an epilogue like nobody else. They are lengthy and heart warming. And this was no different.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Thank you for showing me it was worth taking a gamble again, darling." I dropped my head until my lips were against his and finished, "It feels good finally to win and win huge."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756312._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>The Gamble</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>Series:</b> ✓ <br><b>Reading Order:</b> <br>Book #1 - The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) <br>Book #2 - Sweet Dreams (Colorado Mountain, #2) <br>Book #3 - Lady Luck (Colorado Mountain, #3) <br>Book #4 - Breathe (Colorado Mountain, #4) <br>Book #5 - Jagged (Colorado Mountain, #5) <br>Book #6 - Kaleidoscope (Colorado Mountain, #6)<br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Escape from reality<br>Dark pasts<br>Action/drama<br>Murder mystery<br><b>Warning. This book includes...</b> <br>Sexual content. History of rape. Violence.<br><b>Writing:</b> Fantastic<br><br><a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/The-Gamble-ebook/dp/B004X6TMLA/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1380192494&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=the+gamble" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756313._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/The-Gamble-ebook/dp/B004X6TMLA/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1380192494&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=the+gamble" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756314._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Like this review and want to keep up to date with more book news…?</b><br><blockquote>Follow me at the links below…</blockquote><br>My blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBook...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18085433176732051735">I'm starting to wonder if I'll ever read a KA epilogue and won't have tears in my eyes <3 <br/><br/>This was a re-read, and as much as I remembered how great this book was, I actually didn't remember enough, because this was absolutelyfreakingamazinglyfabulous! It just confirms Colorado Mountain as my favorite KA series <3<br/><br/>The story - I loved the beginning, Nina rents a house in the middle of nowhere, during winter, she gets there, meets Max who essentially throws her out, she gets pissed and ends up with </span>
  <span id="freeText18085433176732051735" style="display:none">I'm starting to wonder if I'll ever read a KA epilogue and won't have tears in my eyes &lt;3 <br /><br />This was a re-read, and as much as I remembered how great this book was, I actually didn't remember enough, because this was absolutelyfreakingamazinglyfabulous! It just confirms Colorado Mountain as my favorite KA series &lt;3<br /><br />The story - I loved the beginning, Nina rents a house in the middle of nowhere, during winter, she gets there, meets Max who essentially throws her out, she gets pissed and ends up with a dead car in the middle of a snowstorm XD Max finds her and nurses her through her cold (oh my that was so adorable &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 ). They hit it off really fast, or should I say, Max forbids her to leave town so she's stuck with him XD And so it goes, they have their ups and downs, fall in love, get kidnapped several times, deal with relatives and former fiancees and girlfriends and so on and so on :) <br /><br />Max - *sigh* oh God he was so sweet and adorable, I just loved him &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 He's not a commando or a badass, just a normal guy, well normal alpha controling guy XD It doesn't take him long to know that Nina is "the one", and he does everything he can to get past her defences and to make them work. That scene when he took her to the bluff *swoons* just beautiful. His part of the epilogue made me cry &lt;3<br /><br />Here's my favorite Max quote, and it sums him up perfectly:<br /><br /><i><br />“You just need to know, I gotta fight to keep what we got so we can build on it, I will.<br />Him, your Dad, you, I don’t give a fuck. In my life, I’ve learned when to let shit go and when to fight. This, babe, what we got, I’ll fight for.” </i><br /><br />Nina - I really liked her :) She goes to America for a timeout from her fiancee who's an idiot if I might say so. Max is great to her, and she reeealy doesn't want to have anything with him, but hey, he's too persuasive XD She's feisty, doesn't let anyone walk all over her, or Max, and she fights with his ex girlfriend and sister (hilarious!!!) It gets ugly for her when she finds out about <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Anna, Max's dead wife who he adored.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I felt bad for her, it's always tough to be in someone's shadow, and that was a major one.<br /><br />All in all, I loved all their moments, some of them were great, some of them beautiful, some very sexy XD some extremely sad :(((<br /><br />A 10+++ rating for this one :)</span>

  <u>Second re-read: 13.08.2019</u>
</b><br/>The thing is, this one is one of the better ones of KA. Max is quite perfect and Nina isn't so annoying as KA's other female characters (though her not talking to Max is annoying). That being said, the book is awfully long, as in; it's too long, and the insta-love is not for me. I mean, a week in and they are talking about moving in. Well, not talking, telling. Overall, I don't regret reading it, but it's too long with little happening in it.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>

    <a title="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea"><img alt="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1390412715p2/3258936.jpg" /></a>

Even when they were being daft or doing something I did not agree with, it was obvious it was borne out of a sense of fear. <br/><br/>Great cast of secondary characters (and as I thought the first time, Brody needs a story!)<br/><br/>Great exciting plot with characters you care about. The writing gives a very real sense of what is happening, and how something is, so you have a very clear picture in your head.<br/><br/>As usual</span>
  <span id="freeText13927553880053460447" style="display:none">Re read - love it as much as the first time.<br /><br />I loved Nina and Max, even with their flaws and issues. <div id="review_1555107549" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1555107549" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1555107549?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=loveable-hero">loveable-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=romantic-funny-hot">romantic-funny-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=funny-hot">funny-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=action-and-romance">action-and-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=fun-tenderness">fun-tenderness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=swoon-worthy-hero">swoon-worthy-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=hero-so-loveable">hero-so-loveable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=alphamale-hero">alphamale-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=fun-banter">fun-banter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=romance-mystery-murder-drama">romance-mystery-murder-drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1555107549" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9735013878378142979"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Well, that was a really long read – nearly 600 pages. Although I quite enjoyed the book, I really think it did not need to be that lengthy. <br/><br/>This is not a romance novel only– it is a mixture of everything. So much stuff happens. Romance, mystery, murder, kidnapping, rape, suicide, cheating, beating... And that was too much after a while. I may enjoy a little bit of action in a romance book but not the overdose like in this one. That was over my limits. Somewhere towards the end, I was ye</span>
  <span id="freeText9735013878378142979" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br>Well, that was a really long read – nearly 600 pages. Although I quite enjoyed the book, I really think it did not need to be that lengthy. <br><br>This is not a romance novel only– it is a mixture of everything. So much stuff happens. Romance, mystery, murder, kidnapping, rape, suicide, cheating, beating... And that was too much after a while. I may enjoy a little bit of action in a romance book but not the overdose like in this one. That was over my limits. Somewhere towards the end, I was yelling at the writer, saying, “Oh my God, enough. She has had enough trauma in her life, aren’t you satisfied?” <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434259._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OK, well, that said, I can say that I still loved the book, but the hero, Max, is the main reason why I loved it. He is a hero I will never ever forget. He easily takes his place in my favorite book boyfriends list.<br><br>Normally, I am not a fan of alpha males. I can accept them only if the dose of possessiveness and dominance is well balanced with compassion and tenderness. They should not be giving orders all the time or they shouldn’t humiliate or hurt women for any reason. Then, I can accept them. But there is a difference between “accepting” someone when you find them tolerable and “loving” them. For me, to be able to love an alpha male, there must be something exceptional about him, the way he shows his love must be one of a kind – somehow special – very very special. <br><br>And, in The Gamble, MAX had it all and more! I loved MAX, and he made me love this book. He made my heart melt. OK, so the bottom line is if he can melt my heart, I can love an alpha male :)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434254._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578220662ra/28713421.gif" width="420" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then, there is our heroine, Nina, or the Duchess, as Max calls her. I had mixed feelings about her. She is cute, sassy and ballsy. She is also witty, compassionate, friendly and funny. However, because of her terrible past relationships, she is insecure and defensive, jumping into conclusions all the time. That is why, the situations that can be resolved easily just by talking becomes a reason for her acting stupid or running away. Her lack of communication with Max about her insecurities is sometimes annoying.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578221386ra/28713481.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, she sometimes sounds annoying because of her one word answers/questions or objections such as “Um...”, “Uh...”, “Max”, “Sorry?”, "I..." etc... She also repeats questions asked to her or repeats what someone has just said to her like a parrot, which is kind of irritating and tiring. Once or twice, it may be OK but again, there is an overdose of it. <br><br>One also questions why she can stand up for herself or for the ones she cares about defending them with enthusiasm using complex and long sentences that will really amaze you with their wit and humor in them but why she stammers like a confused idiot in simpler dialogues. <br><br>*********************************************<br><br>I enjoyed the chemistry between Max and Nina, their bantering and flirting. I loved it when Max called her names like Duchess, Zombi Nina, Sweet Nina etc. I loved how he held her tight and hugged and kissed her so often. I loved how he defended her in all situations. I loved how he remembered the little details about her. I loved how he never let go of her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434256._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story takes place in Colorado Mountains. The views of mountains, cute towns and the mountain cabin were vivid in my mind all along the book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434257._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434258._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The secondary characters were also fun, providing more entertainment. There were a lot of secondary characters, though. And a lot of stuff was happening around them. There were times when I felt like I was watching a soap opera – and not just a few episodes but the full season of it till the finale!<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>I don’t know if people in Colorado speak like that but there was something interesting in the way they spoke. Important words, mostly conjunctions, are missing in some places (especially “if” in conditionals). Some sentences sound kind of incomplete just hanging there. I guess it is the casual way of speaking and although they make sense, they felt grammatically incomplete. Well, I got used to it after a while but that was a drag for me at the beginning.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>Well, talking about the plot is not easy because there are too many details but things more or less revolve around Max and Nina. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578220662ra/28713422.gif" width="420" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515955679ra/24876344.gif" width="420" height="480" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Max had a happy marriage but he lost his wife 10 years ago in a tragic car accident and since then, he never had another woman that he cared about. He just had casual relationships with no commitment.<br><br>Nina is engaged and lives in England although she is American. She is not happy and she needs a timeout before she gets married. She buys a ticket and goes to Colorado Mountains to spend some time alone. There, the problems begin. There has been a mistake in the booking and the house she rented is not available because the owner is staying there at the moment. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434260._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then, things get interesting and they live the forthcoming weeks like on a roller coaster. Max soon realizes that Nina is "the one" – the one he would like to keep for good and he does everything in his power to make her believe that they will be a good couple together. However, it is not only up to them. As things go out of control, they find themselves in the middle of a lot of drama. There is kidnapping, violence and murder.<br><br>Because of the millions of events in the story, it feels never-ending at certain points but I still recommend this book because it is a nice and fun read despite all its flaws and lengthiness. <br><br>It is safe as there is no cheating. Both of them had other partners before. She is 36 and he is 37 years old. However, she is engaged when Nina first meets Max but then, a few days later, she sends her fiancé an e-mail, saying their relationship won't work and breaks up with him. <br><br>She was already on a timeout here in Colorado, thinking her relationship was not good enough for her to marry him. <br><br>Although her (ex)fiancé comes and creates a little drama, I had no problem with it because on her part, it was definitely over. <br><br>A woman Max slept with before also creates a few problems but Max and Nina deal with her brilliantly.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>The writing is good and it makes you feel. I just would prefer it to be less lengthy but still it's good.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>Now, let me present you our main character MAX in all his glory and then, you decide if you would like to read about him:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1578222055i/28713513._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“I dropped my arms and then I slid them around what felt like a man's waist. Then I cuddled closer. It felt like arms came around my waist too, and it also felt like a hand was trailing gently up and down my back.<br>"You're sweet when you're sick."<br>"I am?"<br>"Hellion when you're riled."<br>"Yes?"<br>"Yeah."<br>"Mm."<br>Then he muttered, "Not sure which I like more.” <br><br>***<br><br>“I’m Holden Maxwell,” Max answered immediately, in other words before I could. “I own the house Nina rented. There was a mix up, I had to be in town on personal business and Slim didn’t tell Nina. She showed up at the house and I was there. Lucky I was. She was sick as a dog, lapsed into a fever so bad she was delirious for two days and I was worried I’d have to take her to the hospital. The fever broke and since then things have advanced between us. We’ve gotten to know each other, we both like what we know and, bottom line, you didn’t take care of what was yours. Now, as Nina has explained, you’ve lost it, I found it and it’s mine.”<br><br>***<br><br>“I was your man, you were halfway around the world from me, honey, I'd fuckin' phone you," he said quietly.<br>"Niles is reserved," I whispered.<br>"Niles is an ass," he returned and my brows drew together.<br>"You don't know him."<br>"I know men, and I know he's not reserved, he's an ass."<br>I pulled my head together, my hand from his and snapped, "Yes? And how do you know that?"<br>"Because I've seen you naked, I've seen you sweet, I've seen you unsure and I've seen you riled and, seein' all that, I know, you were half a world away from me, I'd fuckin' phone."<br>"Perhaps that's not the kind of relationship Niles and I have," I suggested snottily, but his words hit me somewhere deep, somewhere I didn't know I had.<br>"You on a timeout?"<br>"What?"<br>"If you told me you needed a timeout, first, I wouldn't fuckin' let you have one, second, I wouldn't give you reason to fuckin' want one, last, you took off anyway, I'd fuckin' phone.” </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434255._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“His hand at my face slid into my hair and his face got close before he said, <br>“I know this. Those assholes are assholes because they did what they did and because they did it to a good woman. Learned some things in my life, Duchess. One of the most important—you find a good woman, you take care of her.” <br>“Please.” <br>“This happens between us, Duchess, I’d take care of you.” <br>“Don’t.” <br>“Die doin’ it,” he vowed.” <br><br>***<br><br>“You just need to know, I gotta fight to keep what we got so we can build on it, I will. Him, your Dad, you, I don’t give a fuck. In my life, I’ve learned when to let shit go and when to fight. This, babe, what we got, I’ll fight for.” <br><br>***<br><br>Niles didn’t bother to look at Mom, he continued to stare at Max. <br>“You’d be a fool to walk away from that,” Dad advised. <br>“What offer?” I asked, looking up at Max. <br>“Your father offered this…” Niles started explaining and my eyes went to him, “ man two hundred and fifty thousand dollars to disappear out of your life. I’m making it three quarters of a million.” <br>I gasped at this news and took a step back but Max’s hand held mine fast, he took a step forward and he was stronger than me so I went with him. He put the knuckles of his fist to the table, leaned toward Niles and spoke quietly, cuttingly, in his rough, gravelly voice:<br> “Fucked her last night, man, and this morning. Five times. Five. It was like she hadn’t been touched in a decade. So fuckin’ sweet. Damn, ” he taunted, his eyes locked on Niles. “You’ve had her, you gotta know, not enough money in the world’s worth that.”<br><br>***<br><br>“Looks like you’re gonna lose it, you do everything you can to stop that from happening.” Max looked back to Niles. “And you didn’t do that. She was a week away from me, she walked into a room I was in holdin’ another man’s hand, I’d lose my fuckin’ mind. Not at her. Wonderin’ where I lost my way and I’d talk to her about how to find my way back”<br><br>***<br><br>“Never," Max said, again ignoring me. "Never did I walk into a room and see her dressed to go out and forget how to breathe like I did when I saw you before we went to The Rooster." I felt my eyes grow wide at this admission and I, too, forgot how to breathe.” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510605955i/24434253._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Originally read in February, 2016<br>Reread in January, 2020</b><br><br>It still felt good when I read it a second time. Max still feels so very swoon-worthy.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578221001ra/28713443.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9735013878378142979" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="WhiskeyintheJar" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2763722-whiskeyinthejar"><img alt="WhiskeyintheJar" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554154693p2/2763722.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2499486046?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="WhiskeyintheJar" class="user" itemprop="url" name="WhiskeyintheJar" href="/user/show/2763722-whiskeyinthejar">WhiskeyintheJar</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2763722-whiskeyinthejar?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2763722-whiskeyinthejar?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2499486046" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7548351624827959900">I've, mostly, given up on Ashley as her writing style/voice more often than not, constantly draws me in with promise but never delivers. This was a Kindle Freebie and Random Number Generator picked it out of the abyss. <br/><br/>This story:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1534876960ra/26173428.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>An Ashley hero calling the heroine "babe" and/or "baby"? NEVER. (She has an English accent so he also calls her Duchess)<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1534876960ra/26173429.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>"Executed a perfect 3 point turn". Why did I read this sentence over and over again? Was Ashley a driver instructor in a former life??<br/><br/><br/>Sandwiched betwe</span>
  <span id="freeText7548351624827959900" style="display:none">I've, mostly, given up on Ashley as her writing style/voice more often than not, constantly draws me in with promise but never delivers. This was a Kindle Freebie and Random Number Generator picked it out of the abyss. <br><br>This story:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1534876960ra/26173428.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>An Ashley hero calling the heroine "babe" and/or "baby"? NEVER. (She has an English accent so he also calls her Duchess)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1534876960ra/26173429.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"Executed a perfect 3 point turn". Why did I read this sentence over and over again? Was Ashley a driver instructor in a former life??<br><br><br>Sandwiched between the "babe" calling, three-point turning, and drama ending was some honest to god deep emotional issues (domestic violence, rape, disabilities) that get broached but never fully developed. Ashley's ability to incorporate these issues and emotions are what tempt me to keep reading her (the promise I was talking about) but ugh, no development. These issues almost start to seem sensationalized and click-bait reading because Ashley doesn't develop the issues and characters. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452271002ra/17671175.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending, my god, the ending. Drama after sensationalized drama. The repeat situations our heroine found herself in got to be tedious and one of the villains ended up being portrayed cartoonish. <br><br> <br>I can see why Ashley is popular and I can see why she in not popular. All I know is, my kingdom for an Ashley hero to speak in full coherent sentences.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7548351624827959900" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_788405105" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/788405105" />
    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/788405105?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=kick-ass-awesome-heroine">kick-ass-awesome-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=my-fictional-boyfriends">my-fictional-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=book-husband">book-husband</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer788405105" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3849042695875113001"><b>*****6+++++ Very Lucky Stars****</b><br/><br/>I really wish <i>The Gamble</i> was like those soap opera TV shows that last for ten years or more, I would happily read about Max and Nina forever and now I'm terribly sad because is over. I must say that Kristen Ashley never does me wrong, this novel was absolute perfection to me.<br/><br/>Nina is an American girl living en England; she has a great job and a beautiful home that was built by her dear brother but her relationship with her fiancé is anything but ideal. He rarely pa</span>
  <span id="freeText3849042695875113001" style="display:none"><b>*****6+++++ Very Lucky Stars****</b><br><br>I really wish <i>The Gamble</i> was like those soap opera TV shows that last for ten years or more, I would happily read about Max and Nina forever and now I'm terribly sad because is over. I must say that Kristen Ashley never does me wrong, this novel was absolute perfection to me.<br><br>Nina is an American girl living en England; she has a great job and a beautiful home that was built by her dear brother but her relationship with her fiancé is anything but ideal. He rarely pays any attention to her and their lives together lacks passion and communication , so before they marry she decides that she needs a time-out and travels back to America in search of a relaxing vacation in the Colorado mountains. When she arrives all odds are against her; there's a snow storm, she's feeling sick with a cold and it turns out the rental she had booked is not really available, but she temporarily forgets all that when she encounters the owner of the cabin, a really big and sexy mountain man named Holden Maxwell, AKA Max.<br><br>Five minutes into the fight with the very fancy and beautiful Nina, Max knew he wanted to get to know this woman and keep her near. Next Nina falls really ill and Max takes her of her for days.They will form a strong bond created by the attraction and the strong feelings neither of them can deny. Max is almost like a the town's hero and Nina's awesome personality will make all the citizens fall in love with her. The romance, the adventure, and the crazy shenanigans will keep Nina and Max together but are they willing to forget the pain from the past and put all their chips down and take a gamble? <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/imagejpg1_zpsd98d2b69.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396488772i/9141843._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zpsd98d2b69.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me tell you that the idea of going on vacation and finding a man as amazing and sexy as Max, makes it for a fantastic plot. Every single time I read a KA novel I get this incredible urge to fly away to Colorado in search of a delicious Alpha Male. I really loved every minute of this novel, the characters had such loyal and unique qualities and this had me feeling all kinds of warm and fuzzy. I know I've said this before but this time I'm dead serious, Max is my #1 book boyfriend and I'm willing to fight anybody for my sexy mountain man...<br><br>Playlist:<br>*There is only one song that I think is perfect for this book:<br>~Be My Forever by Christina Perry Feat. Ed Sheeran. <br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="3849042695875113001" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sUDwRzVr/ohHcjBjZcpTziPurlDGsiKMQEZvXIKJqTqTylE+N9nqOZVVSHwrN+xiXiXnH4swJtnegzZhikcCuw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MggPU8Zv0C8Yxw09V+iw7ix22tCiSZ0B9vt6EDf48wMQgq4qxN3EnsrgdSIZFQ9CUb2Tn+/LmVRoPiMtPzZYgg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer18232068604709259203">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText18232068604709259203" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
